coordinated components:\\n\\n1. **Plugin Process Supervisor and Lifecycle Management** (`pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go`): The Service struct implements the Manager interface to start and stop plugin processes. The `Start` method initializes the plugin process and launches a background goroutine via `startPluginAndKeepItAlive` to manage the plugin lifecycle.\\n\\n2. **Restart Policy on Crash** (`pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go` - `keepPluginAlive` method): Implements automatic plugin restart logic. This function runs in a goroutine with a ticker that checks every second (default) if the plugin process has exited. If the plugin is not decommissioned and has exited, it automatically restarts the plugin using `Start(context.Background())`. This provides automatic recovery for crashed plugins.\\n\\n3. **gRPC Plugin Implementation** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go`): The `grpcPlugin` struct wraps the plugin lifecycle and gRPC communication. It implements Start/Stop methods for process management, maintains plugin state (NotStarted, StartInit, StartSuccess, StartFail, Stopped), tracks the gRPC client connection (`plugin.Client`), and implements the health check handler via `CheckHealth` method that delegates to the gRPC client.\\n\\n4. **gRPC Client Connection Setup** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client.go`): The `newClientConfig` function creates the gRPC client configuration, establishing the connection to the external plugin process. It handles both process mode (direct execution) and container mode (Docker), configures the handshake protocol, versioned plugin support, and OpenTelemetry tracing integration.\\n\\n5. **gRPC Client V2 Implementation** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go`): The `ClientV2` struct implements all gRPC plugin service clients (Diagnostics, Data, Resource, Stream, Admission, Conversion). The `CheckHealth` method (line 141-160) calls the DiagnosticsClient's CheckHealth gRPC method and handles error codes. It also provides the main entry points for plugin communication.\\n\\n6. **Protocol Client Wrapper** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_proto.go`): The `protoClient` provides a higher-level wrapper around the gRPC plugin, implementing the ProtoClient interface and delegating to the underlying `grpcPlugin.getPluginClient` for availability checking before making gRPC calls.\\n\\n7. **Plugin Interface Definitions** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/ifaces.go`): Defines the core Plugin interface with Start, Stop, IsManaged, Exited, CheckHealth, and other methods that all backend plugins must implement.\\n\\n8. **Core Plugin Implementation** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go`): Implements the Plugin interface for built-in Grafana datasources. Core plugins implement health checks through their CheckHealthHandler without requiring gRPC communication.\\n\\n9. **Backend Plugin Provider** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/provider/provider.go`): Uses a provider chain pattern to create appropriate backend plugin factories. plugin processes. The `Start` method initializes the plugin process and launches a background goroutine via `startPluginAndKeepItAlive` to manage the plugin lifecycle.\\n\\n2. **Restart Policy on Crash** (`pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go` - `keepPluginAlive` method): Implements automatic plugin restart logic. This function runs in a goroutine with a ticker that checks every second (default) if the plugin process has exited. If the plugin is not decommissioned and has exited, it automatically restarts the plugin using `Start(context.Background())`. This provides automatic recovery for crashed plugins.\\n\\n3. **gRPC Plugin Implementation** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go`): The `grpcPlugin` struct wraps the plugin lifecycle and gRPC communication. It implements Start/Stop methods for process management, maintains plugin state (NotStarted, StartInit, StartSuccess, StartFail, Stopped), tracks the gRPC client connection (`plugin.Client`), and implements the health check handler via `CheckHealth` method that delegates to the gRPC client.\\n\\n4. **gRPC Client Connection Setup** (`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client.go`): The `newClientConfig` function creates the gRPC client configuration, establishing the connection to the external plugin process.
